<Text>I've played at this course on and off for the last 7 years. I generally enjoy it because the greens are in good condition, the holes are straightforward (no blind shots), the driving range is all grass, and the food in the cafe is pretty good. Additionally, there are at least 5 sets of tees, which means that there is an appropriate set of tees for players of all skills levels. I also appreciate that the design of the course does not snake all the holes parallel to each other, so aside from a few spots (like between 16 green and 17 tee), there is minimal need to duck from screams of "fore!"

I hesitate to give it a full five stars because of the following: the pace of play at times can be pretty slow even with a good chunk of patrons in carts (usually 5 hours +)...and some of the tee boxes could really use some work (especially #12!).< /Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< resp>

< Review>
Playing here again after a long absence. The landscape & topology of the area contribute to a fun, challenging and attractive course (semiprivate). One of the more notable features are the extra large greens that allow so many different pin placements and forcing u to carefully select the right club (don't forget to factor in the wind, today it was upto 2 clubs) The fairway conditions are better than many public courses but still u will still see occasional browned out bare patches. The tee boxes for the most part are in decent condition. The rough is an adequate length to affect your shots. The extra large greens are in good condition  and in combination with the contours and tiers make chipping & putting an interesting conundrum. A scenic and excellent test of golf.< /Review>

<gmap_id>0x80850e997865bbe7:0xae0a835c340daaba</gmap_id><Name>Michael Levy</Name>< Review>
I would like to preface this review by saying I‚Äôve been playing golf for the last 25 years. I‚Äôve played dozens and dozens of courses and feel I have a pretty good gauge on what makes a golfing experience enjoyable. We recently hosted a group outing at Chardonnay Golf Course and we had an outstanding experience. From the ease of organizing this outing with Octavio (he was outstanding to work with) and checking in to carts being set up for us with names labeled on each cart. We had everyone from the single digit handicapper to people who played their very first round of golf on this course that day. Thanks to their kind staff and professional marshal, we were able to introduce the game of golf to people that may have otherwise never played and everyone had a great time. Most people ordered food and were very impressed with the quality. On top of their restaurant being fantastic, they had a food cart on the course on a Tuesday which is amazing in and of itself. The bartender also made great drinks before and after the round. I was very impressed with the quality of the course. Fairways were thick and plush and greens rolled true. It was a very wonderful experience and something we want to do once or twice a year. There‚Äôs no doubt we will be returning to the Chardonnay Golf Club as I don‚Äôt think their quality for the value can be matched in the bay area.<//Review>

< review>
Incredible scenery, excellent conditions from tee to green, great deal on Golf Now app...all made for a great afternoon.  Be prepared for all aspects of your game to be challenged!

Tee boxes, fairways, greens, sand traps...all in excellent condition.  While it's a par 72, it has 6 par 5's, 6 par 4's and 6 par 3's - I love it!  I'm all for variation, and you get it at Chardonnay.  The course winds through vineyards and has multiple elevated tees, which give you incredible, panoramic views.  Take several deep breaths, enjoy the view - even on a day when I wasn't at my best I thoroughly enjoyed this course and definitely want another shot at it!

Here are the challenges:
* Greens: At least 14 of the 18 greens can be considered very narrow, so while distance control issues will be slightly tolerated, left/right misses will not!  Most have several tiers, so the threat of a 3 putt is constant if you don't hit the right level.  But they are fair, smooth and quick...just very challenging.
* Fairways: they are rarely straight, and certainly not wide, so they demand accuracy.  So even though the holes aren't really long, meandering fairways present a whole different challenge.  On par 5's the fairways narrow significantly as you approach the greens, forcing you to be extremely accurate with a fairway wood or lay up with a mid iron.  Experience on this course to know the best spots to land and the trouble you can't see from the tee would be very valuable.
* Distance: Choose your tee level carefully.  Yardage is one thing, but narrow distance is another. 18 is certainly a reachable par 5, but most of the others are not for us mortals but very playable with 3 decent shots.  Most courses have one ore two short par 3's to boost your confidence...not here.  They aren't super long, but they are anything but simple.  Par 4's that are 380-410 yards might not seem too long, but when the landing area isn't straight, and the greens are narrow, those holes just got a LOT tougher.

I didn't see a marshall all day, but we played in 4.5 hours so pace wasn't an issue.  Have a great time, enjoy the challenge!< /review>

I‚Äôm new to golfing, only my 4th time on a course, and I went out with my boyfriend and a friend and a wonderful associate of theirs. It was chilly and foggy out, and we arrived early so our friends could rent some clubs and we could head to the range out front. We were all warmly greeted and renting clubs was a cinch! The gentleman out front got our carts set up promptly and we were on the range within 5 or so minutes. It took a few holes for the fog to start clearing up but when it did, the view of the vineyards were beautiful! The only downside every once in awhile was that the tee boxes were placed a little wonky; one was on the opposite side of the other three, or we found ourselves dropping me off at one while the other guys went almost out of view to tee off.

<Review>Chardonnay Golf Club is one of the most challenging courses to play in Northern California for all skill levels in golf. The staff is extremely friendly and helpful from Head PGA PRO Bob Becker to the Pro Shop staff including administrative staff to the restaurant staff. I chose to make Chardonnay my golf home and joined the club since it really is the best deal you can get for golf in the Napa Valley. I love the course and it is a great place to work on handicapping as well as play in tournaments. The Members Range is great including the Members area where you can work on your game including a private practice green and bunker.
Roger Billings, Director of Golf is who you want to speak with if you are interested in joining this wonderful semi private, non proprietary club. Start your golf membership today at the Chardonnay Club. It is money very well spent if you golf  2 days per week or more.
I love early morning golf since you can see the sunrise to the wild Canadian geese flying around to seeing the mist rise off the ponds of the course while playing in a links  that has characteristics of a Scottish course. You will never be bored here and it will always present you challenge so do manage your game.
Chardonnay Golf Club truly is a gem of the Napa Valley and already I have met many people who come here from all over the world. World Class Wine is not the only offering of the Napa Valley. Golf at the Chardonnay Club is also a World Class Experience and it offers golf and more!<//Review><rating>5</rating>< user_id>
